In particular, I love the contour blush brush. Very versatile and picks up just the right amount of color. Also, the lip pencil is spot on. I don&#x27;t know if it is the cut of the brush or the synthetic hairs but it spreads pigmented color like a dream. Great for OCC Liptars!</li>

However, I wanted to wear makeup for an event I was attending, most notably concealer for under my eyes and a bit of foundation. The problem (for me at least) is that liquid foundation leaves streaks and powder &amp;#34;foundation&amp;#34; looks fake. After a lot of research I decided I needed a brush and was about to purchase quite expensive brushes to get the look that I wanted. However, I decided on these brushes after watching a few videos on YouTube and reading the reviews on this site.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;What&#x27;s great about these brushes is that the packaging tells you which brushes are for what application. For the novice, this simple bit of information is priceless. I used the smallest brush to conceal any dark spots, pimples, etc and the pointed brush to apply concealer around my eyes. These are the best brushes in the kit in my opinion. The largest brush works GREAT for applying all over face/neck foundation. The tip that I followed was to apply the makeup in circular and upward movements. By applying it like this, all of the makeup seeps into your pores and it looks like you aren&#x27;t even wearing any. The flawless look that it gives means I have been wearing makeup more often and I actually enjoy it now.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I seriously can&#x27;t believe how cheap these brushes are. If you are on the fence, I urge you to try them. They work great and are a great intro brush for the average makeup user.</li>

I compared these to my elf studio brushes which are super soft but have the tendency to disperse all the product on the first stroke; these have the ability to retain product and and blend it out while &amp;#34;locking&amp;#34; it in. When I cleaned these and tried to wipe them off, the paper towel I used was still dry because the bristles held in the water! The need to lay a product flat against your face (rather than stippling it in) isn&#x27;t very high priority for me when I&#x27;m trying to put together a natural look.     <li> These brushes are sooo soft and durable. I&#x27;ve had them for a few months now and have definitely roughly washed them with soap, but they still look like new afterwards!!! Great starter brush set for someone, it has all of the essentials and you can substitute the buffing brush for a blush brush. Just make sure that you wash them at least twice a month, especially your foundation brush. Wash the base of the hairs (near the handle) of the foundation brush really well and make sure you spread the hairs apart or else you can have some left over foundation stuck there for months and not even notice it if you don&#x27;t wash it properly- you&#x27;ll a tough time washing it out later on if you don&#x27;t .&lt;br /&gt; Amazing brush set for this price, can &#x27;t really get a better deal.  I even think that the brushes are softer than some MAC brushes of my mom&#x27;s that I&#x27;ve tried before. Only thing that they should fix for future editions, is making the whole handle gold- the black part tends to have foundation stains on there (from my hands) and you have to really scrub it to get it off. Besides that, I would go for it!!!</li>

I clean this brush with my makeup brush sanitary cleaner (the spray/tissue method) daily. Since the brush is so small, I don&#x27;t normally do deep cleanings because I don&#x27;t dip the tips in any product, rather I just smooth the bristles over product in few areas of my face. I like to use UD&#x27;s Optical Blurring Brush. (It&#x27;s ahhh-mazing for liquid foundations!)  So, this poor lil guy just sits in the pouch until I can find some use for it, or maybe if one of my friends wants it.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;All, in all, I do love Real Techniques brushes!  It comes with a pouch, that you can use to sit upright on your counter (Like in the picture of the product), but I&#x27;ve never used it that way. It doesn&#x27;t really seem practical.  I have other ways of storing brushes, like in vanity cups, or my acrylic vanity organizers.  So, like the foundation brush, the pouch is hidden away and doesn&#x27;t get used either.  Another good point to mention about these brushes is the way they are made. They all are pretty round and have a big base with a flat bottom, so when you are applying your makeup and switch to another brush, you can sit the brush upright on your counter and don&#x27;t have to lay it flat. This is good if you plan on using the brush again during the same makeup application so you don&#x27;t have to lay it down with product on and get bacteria, dirt, etc onto the bristles and put it back on your face. Yuk! Who wants that?  All the brushes are also labeled on the handles so you will never forget what kind of brush itis, and they also have Samantha Chapman&#x27;s beautiful signature on the handle in pretty writing.  The colors of the brushes are very beautiful as well! I love the bright golds, pinks, and purples! It makes for a great makeup brush collection!&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;One unfortunate thing about this set is that you can NOT buy these brushes separately! Big Frown! I would prefer if they came in a case like the Sigma brushes, or if they included a cute little bag to keep them in, but that&#x27;s just me. I don&#x27;t like having to put each brush back into a specific place, and I feel like this gets dirty and isn&#x27;t easy to clean.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;I&#x27;ve had the full set of these brushes since they first launched in 2012. Since getting them, I&#x27;ve used at least three of them every single day. That&#x27;s two years of constant use, and they look and preform the same way they did the day I received them. Since getting the full line of these, I have not purchased a single new brush. My old mac brushes lay untouched in the back of my drawer. Not to mention that just one Mac brush costs as much as the whole set of these ones. Did I mention that you can now buy these at Walmart?&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;These brushes are superior to animal hair brushes in every way. They are cruelty free. They are extremely easy to clean-- I timed myself, and I can wash twenty brushes in seven minutes. They do not get stained. I purposely didn&#x27;t clean red OCC Lip Tar off of my lip brush for a month, and the lip tar came off as easily as any other product. (I use Trader Joe&#x27;s Tea Tree Body Wash or just regular Equate hand soap to clean mine.) They  don&#x27;t hold any funky smells or bacteria after washing, since the bristles aren&#x27;t porous, unlike animal hair bristles. For the same reason, they dry off very fast. My RT face brush takes about 30 minutes to dry if I leave it damp on a washcloth, and I can dry it almost completely in a few seconds if I rub the brush against a sham. I&#x27;ve cleaned and dried my brushes right before using them to do my makeup regularly. My mac brushes take hours (sometimes days) to dry completely, even if I wipe them against a sham first. Another advantage of the non-porous bristles is that you don&#x27;t have to condition them. After washing animal hair brushes, you are supposed to condition them with an oil or conditioner so they stay soft and don&#x27;t get brittle. If you don&#x27;t, your brushes will start shedding. The RT brushes don&#x27;t need to be conditioned, and they don&#x27;t shed.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;Then, they are soft. Softer than animal hair. They pick up product and dispense it with ease. Product doesn&#x27;t linger in the brush nearly as much it does on animal hair brushes, which lets me use less product. Truly a pleasure to use and apply makeup with. My one small gripe is that sometimes product can get stuck on the black grip part of these brushes, but that is hardly an issue since it cleans right off. They just might look a bit dirty after rolling around in your makeup bag.&lt;br /&gt;&lt;br /&gt;These are so durable and have held up better than any brush I&#x27;ve ever had before. As I said before, I&#x27;ve beenusing them for two years already and they look and feel the same way they did the day I got them. I&#x27;m sure that they will last for years to come. I would give these to a friend. I would repurchase. Affordable, durable, just a great product. These would be a great gift to anyone that wears makeup. I would recommend these over any other brush on the market. I feel that this is a truly superior product in every way.using them for two years already and they look and feel the same way they did the day I got them. I&#x27;m sure that they will last for years to come. I would give these to a friend. I would repurchase. Affordable, durable, just a great product. These would be a great gift to anyone that wears makeup. I would recommend these over any other brush on the market. I feel that this is a truly superior product in every way.</li>

It sucks. The only time it would be good is if you&#x27;re traveling, but a standard case would work just as well because the stand is lame.  It&#x27;s a good concept but the brushes are really hard to remove from the elastic, especially with their rubberized bases; the case is flimsy, cheap and lightweight, and it would be a PITA to put each brush back in the elastic.  However, I have discovered that people will actually buy these cases on ebay.  So I was able to make a bit of money back on each of the sets I have (this one and the eye set).  The case concept might be a good idea in heavy leather with better quality elastic- then you wouldn&#x27;t have to hold down the case to pull each brush out.</li>
